Hi Everyone,

After quite a bit of deliberation, the contributed talks for the
Singularity User Group (SUG) have been chosen and we are excited to
announce the agenda! We received an outstanding amount of interest for our
first user group and we would like to thank everyone that submitted
proposals.

I have attached the tentative agenda, but please stay up to date by
visiting our website <https://www.eiseverywhere.com/ehome/sug2019/839014/>
as the agenda is subject to change leading up to the event. Registration is
still open, so if you haven't registered yet please make sure to do so. We
look forward to seeing you there!

-- 
Erin Fong
Marketing and Events Coordinator, Sylabs, Inc.
www.sylabs.io
